)@@G@@@@@@@#@@@@@$@@@@[[       SUBROUTINE FORTAB (NAME, LENGTH, TNAME, GEN, ERBX
)@@G@@R, IN, UPNO)                  @@@@[]       PARAMETER SIZE = 8500        BY
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[#           INTEGERBZ
)@@G@@ NAME (2), LENGTH, TNAME, UPNO                                    @@@@[^CA
)@@G@@           LOGICAL GEN, ERR, IN                                         CB
)@@G@@            @@@@[            INTEGER PTR (301), HEAP (SIZE, 3)          CC
)@@G@@                              @@@@[A           INTEGER FIRST6, HASH, HEACD
)@@G@@PPT, STUB, TABSIZ                               @@@@[B                  CE
)@@G@@                                                                  @@@@[BCF
)@@G@@           STUB = IABS (LENGTH - 6) * 6                                 CG
)@@G@@            @@@@[C                                                      CH
)@@G@@                              @@[@[CC          FIND HASH.               CI
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[C                  CJ
)@@G@@                                                                  @@@@[CCK
)@@G@@           FIRST6 = NAME (1)                                            CL
)@@G@@            @@@@[D           FIRST6 = FIRST6 * FIRST6                   CM
)@@G@@                              @@@@[E           HASH = 0                 CN
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[F           HASH = CO
)@@G@@FLD (9, 18, FIRST6)                                               @@@@[GCP
)@@G@@           HASH = MOD (HASH, 301) + 1                                   CQ
)@@G@@            @@@@[H                                                      CR
)@@G@@                              @@[@[HC          SEARCH TABLE.            CS
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[H                  CT
)@@G@@                                                                  @@@@[HCU
)@@G@@           HEAPPT = PTR (HASH)                                          CV
)@@G@@            @@@@[I10         IF (HEAPPT .EQ. 0) GO TO 30                CW
)@@G@@                              @@@@[K               IF (NAME (1) .NE. HEACX
)@@G@@P (HEAPPT, 1)) GO TO 20                         @@@@[M                  CY
)@@G@@ IF (FLD (0, STUB, NAME (2)) .EQ.                                 @@[@[MCZ
)@@G@@     *                 FLD (0, STUB, HEAP (HEAPPT, 2))) GO TO 60        DA
)@@G@@            @@@@[O20             HEAPPT = FLD (18, 18, HEAP (HEAPPT, 3))DB
)@@G@@                              @@@@[P           GO TO 10                 DC
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[Q                  DD
)@@G@@                                                                  @@[@[QDE
)@@G@@C          NOT FOUND.  RETURN IF NO NEW TNAME IS GIVEN.                 DF
)@@G@@            @@@@[Q                                                      DG
)@@G@@                              @@@@[Q30         IF (TNAME .EQ. 0) RETURN DH
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[S           TABSIZ DI
)@@G@@= TABSIZ + 1                                                      @@@@[TDJ
)@@G@@           HEAPPT = TABSIZ                                              DK
)@@G@@            @@@@[U           IF (TABSIZ .LE. SIZE) GO TO 50             DL
)@@G@@                              @@@@[W               WRITE (6, 40)        DM
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[Y40             FORDN
)@@G@@MAT (30X, 'NODETABLE OVERFLOW.  INCREASE HEAP SIZE')              [@D^8TDO
)@@G@@(30X,039HNODETABLE OVERFLOW.  INCREASE HEAP SIZE)     CN)@@@CJ)@@@CL)@@BDP
)@@G@@CK)^39C[)@@@@@@@[Z               ENDFILE 2                              DQ
)@@G@@                              @@@@[)               CALL ERTRAN (6, '@USEDR
)@@G@@ 1,DUMP. . ')                                   ]@^^8>@USE 1,DUMP. .    DS
)@@G@@______@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@DT
)@@G@@@@]@@^@@@@@$@@@@[-               ENDFILE 1                              DU
)@@G@@                              @@@@[+               CALL ERTRAN (6, '@ADDDV
)@@G@@,E 2. . ')                                      ]@#^8!@ADD,E 2. . ______DW
)@@G@@______@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@[<DX
)@@G@@               CALL ERTRAN (6, '@ADD,E 1. . ')                          DY
)@@G@@            ]@#^81@ADD,E 1. . ____________@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@DZ
)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@[=               CALL ERTRAN (3)      EA
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[>               RETEB
)@@G@@URN                                                               @@@@[&EC
)@@G@@50             FLD (18, 18, HEAP (HEAPPT, 3)) = PTR (HASH)              ED
)@@G@@            @@@@[$           PTR (HASH) = HEAPPT                        EE
)@@G@@                              @@@@[*           HEAP (HEAPPT, 1) = NAME (EF
)@@G@@1)                                              @@@@[(           FLD (0,EG
)@@G@@ STUB, HEAP (HEAPPT, 2)) = FLD (0, STUB, NAME (2))                @@@@[%EH
)@@G@@           FLD (0, 18, HEAP (HEAPPT, 3)) = TNAME                        EI
)@@G@@            @@@@[:                                                      EJ
)@@G@@                              @@[@[:C          RETRIEVE STATUS BITS     EK
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[:                  EL
)@@G@@                                                                  @@@@[:EM
)@@G@@60         GEN = .FALSE.                                                EN
)@@G@@            @@@@[?           ERR = .FALSE.                              EO
)@@G@@                              @@@@[!           IN = .FALSE.             EP
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[,           TNAME =EQ
)@@G@@ FLD (0, 18, HEAP (HEAPPT, 3))                                    @@@@[\ER
)@@G@@           FLD (35, 1, GEN) = FLD (33, 1, HEAP (HEAPPT, 2))             ES
)@@G@@            @@@@[0           FLD (35, 1, ERR) = FLD (34, 1, HEAP (HEAPPTET
)@@G@@, 2))                         @@@@[1           FLD (35, 1, IN) = FLD (35EU
)@@G@@, 1, HEAP (HEAPPT, 2))                          @@@@[2                  EV
)@@G@@                                                                  @@[@[2EW
)@@G@@C          PERFORM UPDATES                                              EX
)@@G@@            @@@@[2                                                      EY
)@@G@@                              @@@@[2           GO TO (70, 80, 90, 100), EZ
)@@G@@UPNO                                            @@@@[3                  FA
)@@G@@                                                                  @@@@[3FB
)@@G@@70         GEN = .TRUE.                                                 FC
)@@G@@            @@@@[4           FLD (33, 1, HEAP (HEAPPT, 2)) = 1          FD
)@@G@@                              @@@@[5           RETURN                   FE
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[6                  FF
)@@G@@                                                                  @@@@[6FG
)@@G@@80         ERR = .TRUE.                                                 FH
)@@G@@            @@@@[7           FLD (34, 1, HEAP (HEAPPT, 2)) = 1          FI
)@@G@@                              @@@@[8           RETURN                   FJ
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[9                  FK
)@@G@@                                                                  @@@@[9FL
)@@G@@90         IN = .TRUE.                                                  FM
)@@G@@            @@@@['           FLD (35, 1, HEAP (HEAPPT, 2)) = 1          FN
)@@G@@                              @@@@[;           RETURN                   FO
)@@G@@                                                @@@@[/                  FP
)@@G@@                                                                  @@@@@@FQ
)@@G@@@@#@@ @@@@@^@@@@[/100        RETURN                                     FR
)@@G@@                              @@@@[.                                    FS

)@@G@@TROL FOR EXPRESSION ANALYZER  @[@@@P.     @G@@@P.        THIS ROUTINE SEYN

)@@G@@HE SELECTION IS BASED ON THE TYPE OF SYMBOL AND THE   @B@@@P.        CURYP

)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @F@@@<SDBFNP   EQU   2 .                 BIF CODE -- BIF WITDY
)@@G@@HOUT PARAM  @E@@@<SMRPTR   EQU   4 .                 RESULT OF BIF IS PTDZ

)@@G@@AM LIST ENTRY     @[@@@<.     @E@@@<SMXRPT   EQU   0001 .              PEB
)@@G@@ARAM REPEAT CONTROL BIT @D@@@<SMXSST   EQU   0002 .              SET STREC

)@@G@@APPEARED    @[@@@<.     @C@@@<.              PARAMETER MATCHING CONTROL EF
)@@G@@BYTE  @[@@@<.     @C@@@<SMXNOP   EQU   0 .                 NO MATCHING  EG
)@@G@@@D@@@<SMXSRS   EQU   1 .                 SAVE THE RESULT    @H@@@<SMXEATEH
)@@G@@   EQU   2 .                 EVALUATE AN AGGREGATE TYPE OF THE RESULT   EI

)@@G@@   LINK  SMEXBG . @F@@@<         LOAD  A10,X4 .            INIT. RESULTATT
)@@G@@NT MODE & TYPE    @E@@@<         LOAD  A11,X4 .            SAVE THE RESUTU
)@@G@@LT TO A11   @F@@@<         SLB   A11,2 .             A11 <- (OPD CLASS ATV
)@@G@@ND MODE) * 4@G@@@<         IF    STKBIT,OFF,STKFLG+STKLNG THEN,SMEXD1 . TW
)@@G@@-> NOT COMP RESULT@A@@@<         LOAD  F,STKCL1+STKLNG .    @F@@@<      TX
)@@G@@   LINK  SMEXBG .            GET OPD TYPE AND CLASS OF OPD1 @F@@@<      TY
)@@G@@   LOR   A10,X4 .            EVALUATE RESULT MODE & TYPE    @G@@@<      TZ
)@@G@@   ADD   X4,A11 .            GENERATE BIT PATTERN OF OPD1 AND OPD2@F@@@<UA
)@@G@@         LINK  SMEXOC .            CHECK ON OPD AND OPR COMBI.    @C@@@<UB
)@@G@@         GOTO  SMEXZZ .            -> ERROR     @[@@@<.     @H@@@<.     UC
)@@G@@                             SET THE NEW CLASS AND MODE BIT TO OPD1     UD
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXD2   LABEL .  @A@@@<         LOADA X5,STKSTT+STKLNUE
)@@G@@G .   @E@@@<         LINK  SMXRST .            SET RESULT CLASS AND MODEUF
)@@G@@@^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXRF . @F@@@<SMEXD3   LABEL .                   CUG
)@@G@@ASE OF PTR,FILE,LABEL VARIABLE@D@@@<         IF    STKBIT,ON,STKFLG+STKLUH
)@@G@@NG THEN,SMEXDF .  @E@@@<         IF    SMEXOT,SAME,X6 THEN,SMEXD4 .  -> UI
)@@G@@ASSIGNMENT  @G@@@<         IF    SMEXOE,SAME,X6 THEN,SMEXD4 ELSE,SMEXMX UJ
)@@G@@.  -> .EQ. OR .NE.@[@@@<.     @F@@@<.              TRAVERSING ON STRUC(OUK
)@@G@@PD1) FOR OPERAND TYPE MATCHING@[@@@<.     @B@@@<.        HERE,X6 = OPR TUL
)@@G@@YPE AND CLASS BIT,@C@@@<.             A11= MODE AND CLASS BIT OF OPD1   UM
)@@G@@@#@@@<SMEXD1   LABEL .  @E@@@<         LSDP  X5,STKDSC+STKLNG .  X5 <- SUN
)@@G@@D ADDRESS OF OPD1 @ @@@<         USING SDSECT,X5 .    @F@@@<         SETUO
)@@G@@   SD5SRT,ON,SDCLS5 .  SET STRUCTURE SEARCH STAT BIT  @#@@@<SMEXE1   LABUP
)@@G@@EL .  @F@@@<         IF    SDSTRU,OFF,SDCLS4 THEN,SMEXE2 . -> NOT A STRUUQ
)@@G@@CTURE @D@@@<         LSDP  X5,SDSON .          GO TOWARDS LEAF    @^@@@<UR
)@@G@@         GOTO  SMEXE1 . @#@@@<SMEXE2   LABEL .  @ @@@<         LOAD  F,SUS
)@@G@@DCLS1 .     @F@@@<         LINK  SMEXBG .            GET THE LEAF'S CLASUT
)@@G@@S AND MODE  @F@@@<         LOR   A10,X4 .            EVALUATE RESULTANT UU
)@@G@@MODE & TYPE @G@@@<         ADD   X4,A11 .            GENERATE BIT PATTERUV
)@@G@@N FOR MATCHING    @F@@@<         LINK  SMEXOC .            CHECK ON OPD UW
)@@G@@AND OPR COMBI.    @C@@@<         GOTO  SMEXSE .            -> ERROR     UX
)@@G@@@F@@@<         IF    SD0ART,SAME,STKCL0 THEN,SMEXE3 .  -> ARITH TYPE    UY
)@@G@@@ @@@<         LOAD  A14,SDCLS0 .   @ @@@<         LXOR  A14,STKCL0 .   UZ
)@@G@@@ @@@<         LAND  A14,07,I .     @B@@@<         IF    A14,NZERO THEN,VA
)@@G@@SMEXSE .    @#@@@<SMEXE3   LABEL .  @E@@@<         IF    SDBROT,ZERO THEVB
)@@G@@N,SMEXE4 . -> NO MORE BROTHERS@D@@@<         LSDP  X5,SDBROT .         TVC
)@@G@@RY NEXT BROTHER   @^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXE1 . @#@@@<SMEXE4   LABEL .  VD
)@@G@@@D@@@<         LSDP  X5,SDDAD .          POP UP ONE LEVEL   @C@@@<      VE
)@@G@@   IF    SD5SRT,ON,SDCLS5 THEN,SMEXE5 .   @^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXE3 . VF
)@@G@@@#@@@<SMEXE5   LABEL .  @E@@@<         SET   SD5SRT,OFF,SDCLS5 . CLEAR TVG
)@@G@@HE SEARCH STAT BIT@^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXD2 . @[@@@<.     @D@@@<.     VH
)@@G@@                             ERROR HANDLING     @#@@@<SMEXSE   LABEL .  VI
)@@G@@@F@@@<         LSDP  X5,STKDSC+STKLNG .  RELOAD THE ROOT SD ADDRESS     VJ
)@@G@@@E@@@<         SET   SD5SRT,OFF,SDCLS5 . CLEAR THE SEARCH STAT BIT@F@@@<VK
)@@G@@         GOTO  SMEXSU .            -> ERROR, SET DEFAULT EXPR     @[@@@<VL
)@@G@@.     @[@@@<.     @F@@@<.                                  <VARIABLE> <OVM
)@@G@@P> <VARIABLE>     @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXR4   LABEL .  @C@@@<         LOAVN
)@@G@@DA X5,STKSTT+STKLNG .  CHECK OPD1   @^@@@<         LINK  SMEXFC . @H@@@<VO
)@@G@@         GOTO  SMEXS1 .            -> OPD1 IS LABEL, FILE, OR POINTER VAVP
)@@G@@R     @D@@@<         GOTO  SMEXDF .            -> NOT SCALAR EXPR @#@@@<VQ
)@@G@@SMEXA2   LABEL .  @C@@@<         LOADA X5,STKSTT .         CHECK OPD2   VR
)@@G@@@^@@@<         LINK  SMEXFC . @H@@@<         GOTO  SMEXS3 .            -VS
)@@G@@> OPD2 IS LABEL, FILE, OR POINTER VAR     @D@@@<         GOTO  SMEXDF . VT
)@@G@@           -> NOT SCALAR EXPR @#@@@<SMEXA1   LABEL .  @A@@@<         LOAVU
)@@G@@D  F,STKCL1+STKLNG .    @F@@@<         LINK  SMEXBG .            GET OPDVV
)@@G@@1 CLASS AND MODE BIT    @E@@@<         LOAD  A11,X4 .            SAVE THVW
)@@G@@E BIT INTO A11    @^@@@<         SLB   A11,2 .  @ @@@<         LOAD  F,SVX
)@@G@@TKCL1 .     @F@@@<         LINK  SMEXBG .            GET OPD2 CLASS AND VY
)@@G@@MODE BIT    @G@@@<         ADD   X4,A11 .            ASSEMBLE OPD'S CLASVZ
)@@G@@S AND MODE BITS   @F@@@<         LINK  SMEXOC .            CHECK OPR ANDWA
)@@G@@ OPD COMBINATION  @C@@@<         GOTO  SMEXZZ .            -> ERROR     WB
)@@G@@@F@@@<         IF    SMEXOE,SAME,X6 THEN,SMEXZ1 .  -> OPR IS = OR ^=    WC
)@@G@@@G@@@<         IF    SMEXOR+SMEXOS,ON,X6 THEN,SMEXZ4 ELSE,SMEXRB . *!*!*WD
)@@G@@!*!*!*@#@@@<SMEXZ1   LABEL .  @H@@@<         IF    SMEXCB,OFF,X4 THEN,SMWE
)@@G@@EXZ4 .  -> NOT COMPLEX MODE *!*!*!*!*!    @F@@@<         LOAD  A8,STKOPAWF
)@@G@@ .         LOAD THE OPERATOR'S A-CODE     @F@@@<         IF    A8,EQ,ACRWG
)@@G@@EQ,I THEN,SMEXZ3 .  -> CHANGE BACK TO BIT @E@@@<         IF    A8,NE,ACRWH
)@@G@@NE,I THEN,SMEXZ2 .  -> NOT ^= OPR   @#@@@<SMEXZ3   LABEL .  @C@@@<      WI

)@@G@@I .        CONVERT BACK TO BIT@D@@@<         LINK  EABK1 .             DWK
)@@G@@ELETE OLD TOKEN   @^@@@<         LOAD  A8,A9 .  @#@@@<         PUTC .   WL
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXZ2   LABEL .  @E@@@<         MOVE  STKCL0+STKLNG,SWM
)@@G@@D0STR,I .  SET STRING CLASS   @E@@@<         SET   SDARST,ON,STKCL1+STKLWN
)@@G@@NG .  SET STRING CLASS  @F@@@<         SET   SDRLCX,OFF,STKCL1+STKLNG . WO
)@@G@@RESET REAL/CMPLX BIT    @[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXRF   LABEL .  WP
)@@G@@@F@@@<         IF    SMEXOT,SAME,X6 THEN,SMEXY0 .  -> CURRENT OPR IS := WQ
)@@G@@@#@@@<SMEXY1   LABEL .  @C@@@<         STPOP .                   POP ENTWR

)@@G@@ TO OPD1    @^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXRF . @#@@@<SMEXZ4   LABEL .  @H@@@<WV

)@@G@@L,PTR @#@@@<SMEXS3   LABEL .  @F@@@<         IF    SDARST,ON,STKCL1+STKLXL
)@@G@@NG THEN,SMEXDF ELSE,SMEXS4 .  @[@@@<.     @E@@@<.                       XM
)@@G@@           MULTI-ASSIGNMENT CHECKING@#@@@<SMEXY0   LABEL .  @F@@@<      XN
)@@G@@   LOAD  A14,SMASCC    .     CHECK IF ASSIGN COMMA APPEARED @E@@@<      XO

)@@G@@   A14,1,I .           DECREASE THE COUNTER     @ @@@<         STORE A14XQ
)@@G@@,SMASCC    .@G@@@<         LINK  SMEXEX .            EXCHANGE LEFT VAR AXR
)@@G@@ND EXPRESSION     @E@@@<         STPOP .                   POP UP LEFT HXS
)@@G@@AND VARIABLE@^@@@<         GOTO  SMXOBQ . @[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @[@@@<XT
)@@G@@.     @[@@@<.     @E@@@<.        SMEXR3                     <ARRAY> <OPRXU
)@@G@@> <VARIABLE>@#@@@<SMEXR3   LABEL .  @^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXA2 . @[@@@<XV
)@@G@@.     @[@@@<.     @E@@@<.        SMEXR2                     <VARIABLE> <XW
)@@G@@OPR> <ARRAY>@#@@@<SMEXR2   LABEL .  @E@@@<         IF    SMEXOT,SAME,X6 XX
)@@G@@THEN,SMEXR9 .  -> VAR := ARRAY@F@@@<         LINK  SMEXEX .            EXY
)@@G@@XCHANGE OPD STACK ENTRIES     @^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXR3 . @[@@@<.     XZ
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXR9   LABEL .  @D@@@<         EXERR ERSMAS LEVEL,2 YA
)@@G@@.    ILLEGAL ASSIGNMENT @^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXDF2 .@[@@@<.     @[@@@<YB
)@@G@@.     @#@@@<SMEXR1   LABEL .  @F@@@<         EXERR ERSMX1 LEVEL,2 .    AYC
)@@G@@RRAY STRUCTURE EXPR NOT IT    @D@@@<         GOTO  SMEXDF2 .           -YD
)@@G@@> DEFAULT EXPR    @[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @B@@@<.           YE
)@@G@@   ERROR MESSAGE PRINTING     @#@@@<SMEXZZ   LABEL .  @D@@@<         LOAYF
)@@G@@D  X8,A14 .            MOVE ERROR CODE    @ @@@<         GOTO  *SMEXET,XYG
)@@G@@8 .   @[@@@<.     @E@@@<.              TRANSFER VECTOR FOR ERROR MESSAGEYH
)@@G@@ PRINTING   @#@@@<SMEXET   LABEL .  @F@=@<         + SMEXDF .           YI
)@@G@@     0 - MEXED TYPE EXPRESSIONS     @F@@@=         + SXEXDF .           YJ
)@@G@@     0 - MEXED TYPE EXPRESSIONS     @F@=@<         + SMEXMX .           YK
)@@G@@     1 - ILLEGAL OPERAND/OPERATOR   @F@@@=         + SXEXMX .           YL

)@@G@@           4 - NO. OF DIMENSION UNMATCHED @[@@@=.     @[@@@=.     @[@@@=YP
)@@G@@.     @#@@@=SXEXDF   LABEL .  @D@@@=         LINK  SXSTRG .            XYQ
)@@G@@5-> BCD OF OPER   @ @@@=         EXERR ERSM84 LEVEL,2 @^@@@=         GOTYR
)@@G@@O  SMEXDF2 .@[@@@=.     @[@@@=.     @#@@@=SXEXMX   LABEL .  @D@@@=      YS

)@@G@@M82 LEVEL,2 @^@@@=         GOTO  SMEXDF2 .@[@@@=.     @[@@@=.     @#@@@=YU
)@@G@@SXSTRG   LLOC .   @F@@@=         GOTO *SXSTL,X6 .           X6=OPERATOR YV
)@@G@@TYPE (0 TO 4)     @#@@@=SXSTL    LABEL .  @B@@@=         +SXSTL0 .      YW
)@@G@@            0     @B@@@=         +SXSTL0 .                  1     @B@@@=YX
)@@G@@         +SXSTL1 .                  2 (:=)@B@@@=         +SXSTL0 .      YY
)@@G@@            3     @B@@@=         +SXSTL0 .                  4     @[@@@=YZ
)@@G@@.     @#@@@=SXSTL0   LABEL .  @D@@@=         LOAD  A3,STKOPA .          ZA
)@@G@@ACODE OF OPERATOR @F@@@=         AND,U  A3,077 .            LEAVE INDEX ZB

)@@G@@SXOPNM,A3 .       BCD PTR     @C@@@=         LJMP .                     ZD
)@@G@@-> RETURN   @[@@@=.     @B@@@=SXSTL1   LABEL .                    :=    ZE
)@@G@@@ @@@=         LOADA X5,SXOPAS .    @#@@@=         LJMP .   @[@@@=.     ZF
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXDF   LABEL .  @D@@@<         EXERR ERSZG
)@@G@@M99 LEVEL,2 .    QUIT- EXPR ERROR   @^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXDF2 .@[@@@<ZH
)@@G@@.     @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXMX   LABEL .  @F@@@<         EXERR ERSM20 LEZI
)@@G@@VEL,2 .    ILLEGAL OPERAND/OPERATOR COMB. @^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXDF2 .ZJ
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXIC   LABEL .  @E@@@<         EXERR ERSZK
)@@G@@MCX LEVEL,2 .    ILLEGAL COMPLEX COMPARING@^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXDF2 .ZL
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXSU   LABEL .  @F@@@<         EXERR ERSZM
)@@G@@MSU LEVEL,2 .    STRUCTURE VARIABLE UNMATCHED   @#@@@<SMEXDF2  LABEL .  ZN
)@@G@@@#@@@<         JMP .    @[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMPTRE1  LABEL .  ZO
)@@G@@@ @@@<         LSDP  A8,STKDSC .    @^@@@<         GOTO  SMPTRER .@#@@@<ZP

)@@G@@@E@@@=         EXERR ERMNBS LEVEL,2 . V USSED AS BASED VARIABLE   @^@@@=ZV
)@@G@@         GOTO  SMEXDF2 .@ @@@</.       AUXILIARY SUBROUTINES@[@@@<.     ZW
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @E@@@<.        SUBROUTINE 'SMEXON' GENERATES THE 3 BIT CODE ZX
)@@G@@'XYZ' @F@@@<.        WHICH REPRESENTS CHARACTERISTICS OF THE OPR IN STACZY
)@@G@@K TOP @D@@@<.              X=1 IF STRING OPERATOR, OTHERWISE X=0  @F@@@<ZZ
)@@G@@.              Y=1 IF EQUAL , NOT EQUAL OR := OPR, OTHERWISE Y=0  @E@@@<AA
)@@G@@.              Z=1 IF RELATIONAL OPERATOR, OTHERWISE Z=0    @F@@@<.     AB
)@@G@@   THE RESULT WOULD BE PLACED IN X6. A14 IS USED FOR WORKING@[@@@<.     AC
)@@G@@@#@@@<SMEXON   LLOC .   @E@@@<         LOAD  F,STKOPF .          SET OPRAD
)@@G@@ FLAG TO F-REG.   @E@@@<         IF    SMOPTAF,ON THEN,SMEXO1 .  -> ARITAE
)@@G@@H/STRING OPR@G@@@<         LOAD  X6,SMEXOS,I .       SET STRING OPR CODEAF
)@@G@@ (&,!,NOT,!!)     @#@@@<         LJMP .   @#@@@<SMEXO1   LABEL .  @G@@@<AG
)@@G@@         IF    SMOPTSF,OFF THEN,SMEXO4 .  -> ARITH OPR (+,-,*,/,**)     AH
)@@G@@@E@@@<         LOAD  A14,STKOPP .        LOAD OPERATOR PRECEDENCE @E@@@<AI
)@@G@@         IF    A14,EQ,2,I THEN,SMEXO3 .  -> ASSIGN OPERATOR @C@@@<      AJ
)@@G@@   LOAD  A14,STKOPA .        LOAD A-CODE  @D@@@<         IF    A14,EQ,ACAK
)@@G@@EQ,I THEN,SMEXO2 .  -> OPR =  @D@@@<         IF    A14,EQ,ACNE,I THEN,SMAL
)@@G@@EXO2 .  -> OPR ^= @E@@@<         IF    A14,EQ,ACREQ,I THEN,SMEXO2 .  -> AM
)@@G@@REL. OPR =  @E@@@<         IF    A14,EQ,ACRNE,I THEN,SMEXO2 .  -> REL. OAN
)@@G@@PR ^= @E@@@<         LOAD  X6,SMEXOR,I .       SET RELATIONAL OPR CODE  AO
)@@G@@@#@@@<         LJMP .   @#@@@<SMEXO4   LABEL .  @E@@@<         LOAD  X6,AP
)@@G@@SMEXOA,I .       SET ARITHMETIC OPR CODE  @#@@@<         LJMP .   @#@@@<AQ
)@@G@@SMEXO2   LABEL .  @D@@@<         LOAD  X6,SMEXOE,I .       SET EQ,NE OPRAR
)@@G@@ CODE @#@@@<         LJMP .   @#@@@<SMEXO3   LABEL .  @E@@@<         LOAAS
)@@G@@D  X6,SMEXOT,I .       SET ASSIGNMENT OPR CODE  @#@@@<         LJMP .   AT
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @G@@@<.        SUBROUTINE 'SMEXBG' GENERATES A BAU
)@@G@@IT STIRNG (00, 01, OR 10)     @E@@@<.        WHICH REPRESENTS CLASS AND AV
)@@G@@MODE OF AN OPERAND .    @G@@@<.              SDCLS1 BYTE MUST BE SET TO AW
)@@G@@FLAG REG. BEFORE THIS CALLING @B@@@<.              THE RESULT IS PLACED AX
)@@G@@IN X4.@[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXBG   LLOC .   @B@@@<         IF    SDARST,ONAY
)@@G@@ THEN,SMEXG1 .    @B@@@<         IF    SDRLCX,ON THEN,SMEXG2 .    @D@@@<AZ
)@@G@@         LOAD  X4,SMEXGR,I .       ARITH.REAL  (B'00')@#@@@<         LJMBA
)@@G@@P .   @#@@@<SMEXG2   LABEL .  @D@@@<         LOAD  X4,SMEXGC,I .       ABB
)@@G@@RITH.CMPLX (B'01')@#@@@<         LJMP .   @#@@@<SMEXG1   LABEL .  @D@@@<BC
)@@G@@         LOAD  X4,SMEXGS,I .       STRING.XXXX (B'10')@#@@@<         LJMBD
)@@G@@P .   @[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @F@@@<.        SURBTOUTINE 'SMEXOC' CKECKSBE
)@@G@@ IF THE COMBINATION OF OPR AND@^@@@<.        OPD IS VALID.  @C@@@<.     BF
)@@G@@         X4 : OPERAND MODE AND CLASS BITS @B@@@<.              X6 : OPERBG
)@@G@@ATOR TYPE CODE    @A@@@<.              A14: USED FOR WORKING@[@@@<.     BH
)@@G@@@#@@@<SMEXOC   LLOC .   @F@@@<         LOAD  A14,SMEXOY .        CHECKINBI
)@@G@@G OF BOTH OPD CLASSES   @ @@@<         SRB   A14,0,X4 .     @E@@@<      BJ
)@@G@@   IF    A14,EVEN THEN,SMEXX1 .  -> OPD CLASS ERROR   @F@@@<         LOABK
)@@G@@D  A14,SMEXOZ,X6 .     A14 <- BIT MAP OF OPD.OPR.OPD  @F@@@<         SRBBL
)@@G@@   A14,0,X4 .          SHIFT THE BITS BY THE OPD TYPE @E@@@<         IF BM
)@@G@@   A14,ODD THEN,LJMP1 .   -> VALID COMBINATION  @F@@@<         IF    SMEBN
)@@G@@XOR,SAME,X6 THEN,SMEXX2 .  -> RELATIONAL OPR    @D@@@<SMEXX3   LABEL .  BO
)@@G@@                 OPR/OPD TYPE ERROR @ @@@<         LOAD  A14,SMXTPC,I . BP
)@@G@@@#@@@<         LJMP .   @E@@@<SMEXX1   LABEL .                   MIXED CBQ
)@@G@@LASS EXPRESSIONS  @D@@@<         LOAD  A14,SMXPDC,I .      SET ERROR CODBR
)@@G@@E     @C@@@<         LJMP .                    ERROR RETURN @#@@@<SMEXX2BS
)@@G@@   LABEL .  @F@@@<         IF    SMEXGS,ON,X4 THEN,SMEXX3 .  -> CLASSES BT
)@@G@@ARE STRING  @F@@@<         LOAD  A14,SMXICC,I .      SET ILL.COMPLX COMPBU
)@@G@@ARE CODE    @C@@@<         LJMP .                    ERROR RETURN @[@@@<BV
)@@G@@.     @E@@@<SMEXOY   + 02063 .                 OPERAND CLASS CHECK BITS BW
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @E@@@<SMEXOZ   + 00063 .                 ARITHMETIC(+,-,*,/,BX
)@@G@@**)   @E@@@<         + 02001 .                 RELATIONAL(>,>=,<,<=)    BY
)@@G@@@F@@@<         + 02063 .                 ASSIGNMENT(:=,ASSIGNMENT COMMA)BZ

)@@G@@.        SUBROUTINE SMEXEX    @F@@@<.              EXCHANGE TOP AND NEXTCC
)@@G@@ ENTRIES OF OPERAND STACK     @C@@@<.              A13 AND A14 ARE USED CD
)@@G@@FOR WORKING @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXEX   LLOC .   @D@@@<         LOAD  A13CE
)@@G@@,STKSTT .        SAVE STKSTT[OPD2]  @F@@@<         MOVE  STKSTT,STKSTT+SCF
)@@G@@TKLNG .  STKSTT[OPD2]<-STKSTT[OPD1] @F@@@<         STORE A13,STKSTT+STKLCG
)@@G@@NG . STKSTT[OPD1]<-OLD STKSTT[OPD2] @F@@@<         LOADD A13,STKCLS .   CH
)@@G@@     STKCLS[OPD2]<-STLCLS[OPD1]     @G@@@<         MOVE  STKCLS,STKCLS+SCI

)@@G@@LS+STKLNG .  STKCLS[OPD1]<-OLD STKCLS[OPD2]     @C@@@<         LJMP .   CK
)@@G@@                 -> RETURN    @[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @ @@@<.        SUBCL

)@@G@@.     @ @@@<.        SUBROUTINE SMEXBC    @F@@@<.              CHECK IF CQ

)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @ @@@<.        SUBROUTINE  SMEXDM   @C@@@<.              COMCZ

)@@G@@ROUTINE  SMXTSD   @F@@@<.              DECIDES A TYPICAL SD IN AN EXPRESDH
)@@G@@SION, AND KEEPS   @F@@@<.              THE B-CODE ADDRESS AND TYPE INTO DI
)@@G@@SMXSTP AND SMXDMP,@ @@@<.              RESPECTIVELY.  @[@@@<.     @#@@@<DJ
)@@G@@SMXTSD   LOCAL .  @F@@@<         IF    SMTSDE,NSAME,SMXARP THEN,JMP .  -DK

)@@G@@ THE SD     @#@@@<         JMP .    @[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @ @@@<.     DR
)@@G@@   SUBROUTINE  SMEXFC   @E@@@<.              CHECKS IF THE OPERAND HAS ADS
)@@G@@ SCALAR VALUE .   @E@@@<.              X5 -- THE ADDRESS OF THE OPERAND DT
)@@G@@STACK ENTRY @B@@@<.              X8, A7 -- USED FOR WORKING @G@@@<.     DU
)@@G@@         IF THE OPD IS A LABEL, FILE, OR POINTER VAR, THEN RETURN @B@@@<DV
)@@G@@.              TO THE NEXT INSTRUCTION    @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXFC   LLODW
)@@G@@C .   @ @@@<         USING STKDS,X5 .     @F@@@<         IF    STKMVR,NSDX
)@@G@@AME,STKMOD THEN,SMEXF9 .  -> NOT SCALAR   @E@=@<         IF    SD3ARE,ONDY
)@@G@@,STKCL3 THEN,SMEXF9 .  -> AREA VAR  @E@@@=.        IF    SD3ARE,ON,STKCLDZ

)@@G@@         GOTO  *SMEXFJ,A3 .   @[@@@<.     @D@@@<.              TRANSFER EB
)@@G@@VECTOR FOR EACH OPD CLASS     @[@@@<.     @D@@@<SMEXFJ   + SMEXF9 .     EC
)@@G@@           0 NONE (ERROR)     @C@@@<         + SMEXF1 .                1ED
)@@G@@ ARITHMETIC @B@@@<         + SMEXF2 .                2 ENTRY@D@@@<      EE
)@@G@@   + SMEXF9 .                3 STRUCTURE (ERROR)@C@@@<         + SMEXF1 EF
)@@G@@.                4 STRING     @C@@@<         + SMEXF0 .                5EG
)@@G@@ LABEL .    @B@@@<         + SMEXF0 .                6 FILE @C@@@<      EH
)@@G@@   + SMEXF0 .                7 POINTER    @C@@@=         + SMEXF0 .     EI
)@@G@@           8 IGNORE     @B@@@=         + SMEXF9 .                9 AREA EJ
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXF9   LABEL .  @D@@@<         LJMP  1 .            EK
)@@G@@     -> ERROR RETURN    @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMEXF0   LABEL .  @C@@@<      EL
)@@G@@   LJMP  .                   OTHERWISE    @[@@@<.     @C@@@<SMEXF2   LABEM
)@@G@@EL .                   ENTRY NAME   @C@@@<         IF    STKSLT,ON,STKFLEN
)@@G@@G THEN,SMEXF4 .   @ @@@<         LSDP  X8,STKDSC .    @ @@@<         USIEO
)@@G@@NG SDSECT,X8 .    @F@@@<         IF    SDBLUS,ON,STKCL1 THEN,SMEXF5 .  -EP
)@@G@@> USER FUNCTION   @G@@@<         IF    SDBFNP,NSAME,SDBFSC THEN,SMEXF9 .EQ
)@@G@@  -> BIF FUNC WITH ARG'S@G@@@<         IF    SD4PVA,ON,SDCLS4 THEN,SMEXFER
)@@G@@7 .  -> P.V WITHOUT PARAM     @#@@@<SMEXF6   LABEL .  @D@@@<         SETES
)@@G@@   SMXFCL,ON,DSMFLG .  SET F. CALL BIT ON @E@@@<         SET   STKBIT,ONET
)@@G@@,STKFLG .  SET COMP REULST BIT ON   @^@@@<         GOTO  SMEXF4 . @E@@@<EU
)@@G@@SMEXF5   LABEL .                   USER FUNCTION REFERENCE  @F@@@<      EV
)@@G@@   IF    SDPARM,ON,SDCLS2 THEN,SMEXF4 .  -> ENTRY PARAMETER @G@@@<      EW
)@@G@@   IF    SDNARG,ZERO THEN,SMEXF6 ELSE,SMEXF9 .  -> NO. OF ARG ZERO@#@@@<EX
)@@G@@SMEXF7   LABEL .  @D@@@<         SET   SMXPSV,ON,DSMFLG .  SET P.V. REF EY
)@@G@@BIT ON@G@@@<         IF    SMRPTR,NSAME,SDBFSR THEN,SMEXF4 .  -> RESULT EZ
)@@G@@IS NOT PTR  @D@@@<         MOVE  STKCL0,SD0PTR,I .  SET PTR TO THE ENTRYFA
)@@G@@@B@@@<         LJMP  2 .                 RETURN @#@@@<SMEXF4   LABEL .  FB
)@@G@@@E@@@<         LOAD  A7,SD0ART,I .       SET ARITHMETIC RESULT    @E@@@<FC

)@@G@@@E@@@<         STORE A7,STKCL0 .         STORE THE CLASS CODE     @#@@@<FF
)@@G@@SMEXF1   LABEL .  @C@@@<         LJMP  2 .                 NORMAL RETURNFG
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @ @@@<.        SUBROUTINE  SMXRST   @F@@@<.     FH
)@@G@@         UPDATES OPD STACK ENTRY TO REFLECT THE OPERATION   @E@@@<.     FI
)@@G@@         PERFORMED ON THE OPERANDS IN THE STACK .     @F@@@<.           FJ
)@@G@@   SDRLCX AND SDARST BITS IN STKCL1 BYTE ARE SET.     @F@@@<.           FK
)@@G@@   ASSUME :  X5 -- THE OPERAND STACK ENTRY ADDRESS    @C@@@<.           FL
)@@G@@             X6 -- THE OPERATOR CODE@E@@@<.                        A10 -FM
)@@G@@ RESULT CLASS AND MODE BITS   @B@@@<.                         F -- WORKIFN
)@@G@@NG    @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMXRST   LLOC .   @ @@@<         USING STKDS,X5 FO
)@@G@@.     @F@@@<         IF    SMEXOR,ON,X6 THEN,SMXRS1 .  -> RELATIONAL OPEFP
)@@G@@RATION@^@@@<         LOAD  F,A10 .  @F@@@<         IF    SMEXGS,ON THEN,FQ
)@@G@@SMXRS1 .  -> RESULT IS STRING CLASS @F@@@<         IF    SMEXGC,OFF THENFR
)@@G@@,LJMP .  -> RETURN IF REAL MODE     @E@@@<         SET   SDRLCX,ON,STKCLFS
)@@G@@1 .  SET COMPLEX MODE BIT     @#@@@<         LJMP .   @#@@@<SMXRS1   LABFT
)@@G@@EL .  @E@@@<         MOVE  STKCL1,SDARST,I .   SET STRING CLASS BIT     FU
)@@G@@@#@@@<         LJMP .   @[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @ @@@<.        SUBROUTINFV
)@@G@@E  SMAGMD   @G@@@<.              EVALUATES AN AGGREGATE CLASS AND MODE OFW
)@@G@@F A BIF PARAM     @E@@@<.              THE RESULT IS SET IN F-REG.  THE FX
)@@G@@MEANING IS  @D@@@<.                   '00'B -- ALL ELM'S ARE REAL MODE  FY
)@@G@@@H@@@<.                   '01'B --     ''    ARE COMPLEX MODE (REAL MIGHFZ
)@@G@@T BE MIXED) @D@@@<.                   '10'B --     ''    STRING CLASS   GA
)@@G@@@D@@@<.              X4,X5,A10, AND A11 ARE USED FOR WORKING@[@@@<.     GB
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMAGMD   LOCAL .  @ @@@<         USING STKDS,X7 .     GC
)@@G@@@ @@@<         LOAD  X5,STKMOD .    @ @@@<         GOTO  *SMAGMJ,X5 .   GD
)@@G@@@B@@@<SMAGMJ   + SMAGME .                0 ERROR@E@@@<         + SMAGMV GE
)@@G@@.                1 VARIABLE (SCALAR EXPR) @B@@@<         + SMAGMA .     GF
)@@G@@           2 ARRAY@C@@@<         + SMAGMS .                3 STRUCTURE  GG
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMAGME   LABEL .  @C@@@<         JMP .                GH

)@@G@@ ADDRESS    @F@@@<         LINK  SMEXFC .            CHECK IF THE OPD ISGK
)@@G@@ SCALAR     @E@@@<         GOTO  SMAGME .            ->  POINTER, FILE NGL
)@@G@@AME   @C@@@<         GOTO  SMAGME .            -> NOT SCALAR@D@@@<SMAGMAGM
)@@G@@   LABEL .                   ARRAY EXPRESSION   @ @@@<         LOAD  F,SGN
)@@G@@TKCL1 .     @F@@@<         LINK  SMEXBG .            GET OPD CLASS AND TGO
)@@G@@YPE BITS    @^@@@<         LOAD  F,X4 .   @#@@@<         JMP   1 .@[@@@<GP
)@@G@@.     @[@@@<.     @E@@@<SMAGMS   LABEL .                   STRUCTURE EXPGQ
)@@G@@RESSION     @F@@@<         IF    STKBIT,ON,STKFLG THEN,SMAGMA .  -> COMPGR
)@@G@@ RESULT     @E@@@<         MOVE  A10,0,I .           INIT. AGGREGATE MODGS
)@@G@@E     @E@@@<         MOVE  A11,0,I .           INIT. AGGREGATE CLASS    GT
)@@G@@@F@@@<         LSDP  X5,STKDSC .         X5 <- SD ADDR OF THE STRUC ROOTGU
)@@G@@@ @@@<         USING SDSECT,X5 .    @E@@@<         SET   SD5SRT,ON,SDCLSGV
)@@G@@5 .  SET A TRAVERSE START BIT @#@@@<SMAGM1   LABEL .  @F@@@<         IF GW
)@@G@@   SDSTRU,OFF,SDCLS4 THEN,SMAGM2 .  -> NOT A STRUCTURE@E@@@<         LSDGX
)@@G@@P  X5,SDSON .          SET THE SON'S ADDRESS    @D@@@<         GOTO  SMAGY
)@@G@@GM1 .            GO TOWARDS LEAF    @F@@@<SMAGM2   LABEL .              GZ
)@@G@@     THE CASE OF REACHING A LEAF    @D@@@<         LOR   A11,SDCLS0 .   HA
)@@G@@     CUMULATE CLASS     @ @@@<         LOAD  F,SDCLS1 .     @G@@@<      HB
)@@G@@   LINK  SMEXBG .            GET CLASS & MODE BITS OF THE ELM     @C@@@<HC

)@@G@@@F@@@<         IF    SDBROT,ZERO THEN,SMAGM3 .  -> NO MORE BROTHERS     HE
)@@G@@@E@@@<         LSDP  X5,SDBROT .         GO TO THE NEXT BROTHER   @^@@@<HF
)@@G@@         GOTO  SMAGM1 . @#@@@<SMAGM3   LABEL .  @D@@@<         LSDP  X5,HG
)@@G@@SDDAD .          BACK TO THE PARENT @F@@@<         IF    SD5SRT,OFF,SDCLHH
)@@G@@S5 THEN,SMAGM4 .  -> MORE PARENTS   @F@@@<         SET   SD5SRT,OFF,SDCLHI
)@@G@@S5 . RESET A TRAVERSE START BIT     @D@@@<         LAND  A11,07,I .     HJ
)@@G@@     EXTRACT CLASS BITS @C@@@<         IF    SD0ART,SAME,A11 THEN,SMAGM6HK
)@@G@@ .    @C@@@<         IF    SD0STR,NSAME,A11 THEN,SMAGME .   @#@@@<SMAGM6HL
)@@G@@   LABEL .  @D@@@<         LOAD  F,A10 .             SET THE RESULT     HM
)@@G@@@F@@@<         SET   STKBIT,ON,STKFLG .  SET THE COMP RESULT BIT ON     HN
)@@G@@@E@@@<         IF    SMEXGS,OFF THEN,SMAGM5 .  -> NOT STRING CLASS@E@@@<HO

)@@G@@   JMP   1 .@#@@@<SMAGM5   LABEL .  @F@@@<         IF    SMEXGC,OFF THENHQ
)@@G@@,JMP1 .  -> RETURN IF REAL MODE     @D@@@<         MOVE  STKCL1,SDRLCX,IHR
)@@G@@ .   SET COMPLEX BIT ON @#@@@<         JMP   1 .@[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     HS
)@@G@@@ @@@<.        SUBROUTINE  SMCLSC   @[@@@<.     @G@@@<.              MATHT
)@@G@@CHING TWO OPERAND'S CLASSES IF THEY ARE CONSISTENT    @D@@@<.           HU
)@@G@@             A13 - FIRST OPERAND SDCLS0   @D@@@<.                       HV
)@@G@@ A14 - SECOND OPERAND SDCLS0  @F@@@<.              IF ERROR DETECTED, THHW
)@@G@@EN RETURN TO THE NEXT INSTR   @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMCLSC   LLOC .   @^@@@<HX
)@@G@@         LXOR  A13,A14 .@E@@@<         LAND  A13,07,I .          LEAVE CHY
)@@G@@LASS BIT ONLY     @D@@@<         IF    A13,NZERO THEN,LJMP .  -> UNMATCHHZ

)@@G@@   IF    SD0STR,SAME,A14 THEN,LJMP1 .  -> STRING@F@@@<         IF    SMEIC
)@@G@@XOT,SAME,X6 THEN,LJMP1 .  -> ASSIGNMENT OPERATOR@G@@@<         IF    SMEID
)@@G@@XOE,SAME,X6 THEN,LJMP1 ELSE LJMP .  -> RELATIONAL OPT @B@@@</.          IE
)@@G@@   NAME RESOLVING SUBROUTINES @[@@@<.     @[@@@<.     @A@@@<.           IF
)@@G@@   SUBROUTINE  SMRSOU   @G@@@<.              RESOLVES A NAME AND OUTPUT IG
)@@G@@THE SD POINTER INTO B-CODE    @[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMRSOU   LOCAL  . @ @@@<IH
)@@G@@         USING STKDS,X7 .     @F@@@<         IF    ACSTAR,SAME,STKTPE THII
)@@G@@EN,SMRSOW .  -> * IN EXPR     @H@@@<         IF    STKMVF,ON,STKFLG THENIJ
)@@G@@,JMP1 . -> RETURN IF ALREADY RESOLVED     @C@@@<         LINK  SMRSLV . IK
)@@G@@           RESOLVE SD   @E@@@<         GOTO  SMRSOV .            -> SD RIL
)@@G@@ESOLUTION ERROR   @#@@@<SMRSOW   LABEL .  @ @@@<         LSDP  A8,STKTPEIM
)@@G@@ .    @E@@@<         PUTC .                    OUTPUT SD PTR INTO B-CODEIN
)@@G@@@E@=@<         MOVE  STKFLG,STKMVF,I .   SET SD MOVED INDICATOR ON@E@@@=IO
)@@G@@         SET   STKMVF,ON,STKFLG .    SET SD MOVED INDIC. ON @C@@@<      IP
)@@G@@   JMP   1 .                 -> RETURN    @#@@@<SMRSOV   LABEL .  @D@@@<IQ
)@@G@@         JMP .                     -> ERROR RETURN    @[@@@<.     @[@@@<IR
)@@G@@.     @ @@@<.              NAME RESOLVER  @[@@@<.     @C@@@<.        X7=IS
)@@G@@STACK TOP (LOWEST PART OF NAME)     @C@@@<.        ADJUSTS STACK TO POINIT
)@@G@@T TO SD (NOT BCD) @C@@@<.        RETURNS AT $+0=ERROR,   $+1=FOUND SD   IU
)@@G@@@[@@@<.     @#@@@<SMRSLV   LOCAL .  @D@@@<         LOADA X9,SMRSS1-1 .  IV
)@@G@@     SET TO STATE 1     @C@@@<         LOAD  F,4,I .             SET FLAIW
)@@G@@G     @D@@@<         LOAD  A8,0,I .            SET LEVEL OF RESULT@C@@@<IX
)@@G@@         MOVE  DSMRSD,0,I .        SET TO NO SD @ @@@<         USING SDBIY
)@@G@@CD,X4 .     @E@@@<         LSDP  X4,STKTPE .         GET BCD PTR FOR FIRIZ
)@@G@@ST SD @F@@@<         IF    0400,ON,SDBCL4 THEN,JMP1 . -> SD, NOTHING TO JA
)@@G@@DO    @ @@@<         USING SDSECT,X4 .    @#@@@<SMRS01   LABEL .  @D@@@<JB
)@@G@@         LOAD  X4,SDBDLK .         GET NEXT SD ADDR   @F@@@<         IF JC
)@@G@@   X4,ZERO THEN,SMRSDN .    -> LAST SD, CHECK RESULTS @D@@@<         LOAJD
)@@G@@D  X5,SDBKLK .         SEE IF BLOCK ACTIVE@ @@@<         USING SDSECT,X5JE
)@@G@@ .    @G@@@<         IF    1,ON,SDBKAC THEN,SMRS01X . -> BLOCK ACTIVE, TJF
)@@G@@RY NEXT SD  @D@@@<         LOAD  A3,DSMD .         SEE IF CHECK EXPR    JG
)@@G@@@F@@@<         IF    A3,NE,ICDYCY,I THEN,SMRS01 .  -> NOT CHECK, NEXT SDJH
)@@G@@@#@@@<SMRS01X  LABEL .  @D@@@<         LINK  SMRSSD .            SEE IF JI
)@@G@@IT RESOLCES @D@@@<         GOTO  SMRS02 .            -> NO, TRY NEXTSD  JJ
)@@G@@@E@@@<         ADD   X5,X9 .             GET STATE TABLE ENTRY    @^@@@<JK
)@@G@@         GOTO  *0,X5 .  @E@@@<SMRSFQ   LABEL .                   FULLY QJL
)@@G@@UALIFIED REUSLT   @ @@@<         USING SDSECT,X4 .    @D@@@<         LOAJM
)@@G@@DA X9,SMRSS2-1 .       SET TO STATE 2     @C@@@<         LOAD  F,1,I .  JN
)@@G@@           SET FQ FLAG  @#@@@<SMRSF2   LABEL .  @C@@@<         STORE X4,JO
)@@G@@DSMRSD .         SET RESULT SD@C@@@<         LOAD  X5,SDBKLK .         GJP
)@@G@@ET BLOCK    @D@@@<         LOAD  A7,SDBKDP,X5 .      GET BLOCK DEPTH    JQ
)@@G@@@#@@@<SMRS02   LABEL .  @F@@@<         IF    SD4PVA,OFF,SDCLS4 THEN,SMRSJR
)@@G@@01 .  -> NOT PSEUDO VAR @D@@@<         LOAD  X4,SDBDLK .         GET BIFJS
)@@G@@ SD ADDR    @C@@@<         GOTO  SMRS01 .            TRY NEXT SD  @#@@@<JT
)@@G@@SMRSNF   LABEL .  @C@@@<         LOAD  F,2,I .             SET TO NFQ   JU
)@@G@@@C@@@<         LOADA X9,SMRSS3-1 .       SET STATE 3  @C@@@<         GOTJV
)@@G@@O  SMRSF2 .            SET RESULT SD@D@@@<SMRSAB   LABEL .              JW
)@@G@@     AMBIGUOUS REFERENCE@C@@@<         SET   0010,ON .           SET FLAJX
)@@G@@G     @C@@@<         GOTO  SMRS02 .            -> NEXT SD   @#@@@<SMRSFQJY
)@@G@@2  LABEL .  @C@@@<         LOAD  X6,SDBKLK .         GET BLOCK SD @ @@@<JZ
)@@G@@         USING SDSECT,X6 .    @E@@@<         IF    A7,LT,SDBKDP THEN,SMRKA
)@@G@@SFQ .   DEEPER BLOCK    @G@@@<         IF    A7,EQ,SDBKDP THEN,SMRSAB . KB
)@@G@@  -> SAME LEVEL, AMBIGUOUS    @B@@@<         GOTO  SMRS02 .            IKC
)@@G@@GNORE @C@@@<SMRSDN   LABEL .                   NO MORE SD'S @E@@@<      KD
)@@G@@   IF    0010,OFF THEN,SMRSD1 .       NOT AMBIGUOUS   @B@@@<         LSDKE
)@@G@@P  A8,DSMRSD           . ERROR@A@@@<         EXERR ERSM01 LEVEL,1 .     KF
)@@G@@@^@@@<         GOTO  SMRSD7 . @C@@@<SMRSD4   LABEL .                   PKG
)@@G@@OP NAME     @E@@@<         IF    STKQNS+STKLNG,ZERO THEN,SMRSD5 .    -> KH
)@@G@@END   @C@@@<         STPOP .                   POP STACK    @^@@@<      KI
)@@G@@   GOTO  SMRSD4 . @#@@@<SMRSD5   LABEL .  @D@@@<         STPOP .        KJ
)@@G@@           POP LAST ELEMENT   @^@@@<         JMP . RETURN   @#@@@<SMRSD1KK
)@@G@@   LABEL .  @C@@@<         IF    03,ON THEN,SMRSD7 . -> SOME QUAL @#@@@<KL
)@@G@@SMRSD0   LABEL .  @ @@@<         LOAD  A8,STKTPE .    @C@@@<         EXEKM
)@@G@@RR ERSM02 LEVEL,2 . NO QUAL OF NAME @^@@@<         GOTO  SMRSD4   @#@@@<KN

)@@G@@SMRSE2   LABEL .  @G@@@<         IF    0100,ON,DSMFLG THEN,SMRSE3 .  -> LT

)@@G@@SMRSS1   LABEL .                   STATE 1 - START    @D@@@<         +SMMC

)@@G@@     DELETE PREFIX BCODE FLAG @B@@@@         LJMP .                    RQY
)@@G@@ETURN @G@@@@SASRCH   LLOC .                    SEARCH FOR LOWER LEVEL INQZ
)@@G@@ NEST WITHOU@D@@@@         LOAD  X5,DSISWL .         ELSE . GET LEVEL   RA
)@@G@@@#@@@@SASRH4   LABEL .  @ @@@@         USING STSBLK,X5 .    @C@@@@      RB
)@@G@@   BINDZ STIEI,SASRH8 .      -> NO 'ELSE' @D@@@@         BINDZ STIBI,SASRC

)@@G@@@#@@@@SASRH8   LABEL .  @C@@@@         STORE X5,DSISWL .         SET NEWRF
)@@G@@ LEVEL@E@@@@         SET   1,ON,DSPFXN .       ALLOW 'ELSE' ON NEXT STMTRG
)@@G@@@D@@@@         IF    STICI,ZERO THEN,LJMP . ->NOT CASE STMT @C@@@@      RH
)@@G@@   SET   0100,ON,DSPFXN . ->ALLOW \N\ NEXT@F@@@@         LJMP .         RI
)@@G@@                              -> RETURN   @F@@@@SATENT*  LLOC .         RJ
)@@G@@           CHECK FOR ELSE ON ILLG STMT    @B@@@@.              IF THEN, RK
)@@G@@NULL STMT INSERTED@E@@@@.                                  IF ELSE, IT IRL

)@@G@@         AND,U A7,012 .            CHECK THEN OR ELSE            *******RN
)@@G@@@F@@@@         IF    A8,EQ,0,I THEN,LJMP . -> NO THEN OR ELSE, RETURN   RO
)@@G@@@G@@@@         AND,U A7,010 .            CHECK FOR THEN .              *RP

)@@G@@.        INSET NULL STATEMENT @C@@@@         STACK X11 .               SRR
)@@G@@AVE REUTN   @^@@@@         USING WORD,X7 .@C@@@@         SAERR SAEM35,SARS
)@@G@@E .       MISSING ;     @C@@@@         SAERR SAEM41,SAE .       MISSING RT

)@@G@@   JMP .                     -> RETURN    @[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @D@@@@RV
)@@G@@SANLST*  LOCAL .                    SET NULL STMT     @D@@@@         MOVRW

)@@G@@@D@@@@         LINK  SASTEN .             END CURRENT STMT  @D@@@@      RZ

)@@G@@IX ORDER    @D@@@@SAEB06*  SAERL SAEM06,SAESE .      IMPROPER CONDITION TS

)@@G@@A STANDARD FORM.  @B@@@@ THERE ARE THREE FORMS OF B CODE TOKENS.  @[@@@@VX
)@@G@@SPACE @F@@@@         1. OPERATORS. THESE ARE THE 18 BIT ALPHA CODES GENEVY
)@@G@@RATED @D@@@@ BY LEXI. THEY ARE IN THE RANGE 0200000 TO 0377777.   @[@@@@VZ
)@@G@@SPACE @F@@@@         2. OPERANDS. THESE ARE 18 BIT POINTERS TO SYMBOL TAWA
)@@G@@BLE   @F@@@@ ENTRIES. THEY ARE IN THE RANGE 0 TO 0177777; SO THEY CAN BEWB
)@@G@@ DI-  @B@@@@ STINGUISHED FROM ALPHA CODE OPERATORS.   @[@@@@SPACE @G@@@@WC
)@@G@@         NOTE. PLUM WILL RUN IN AT MOST 65K CORE. 16 BIT ADDRESSING     WD
)@@G@@@C@@@@ IS ASSUMED FOR ALL SYMBOL TABLE REFERENCES.    @[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@WE
)@@G@@         3. POINTERS. POINTERS ARE 18 BIT OPERANDS THAT POINT TO  @F@@@@WF
)@@G@@ OTHER B CODE ADDRESSES. THESE POINTERS ARE  DISTINGUISHED FROM   @A@@@@WG
)@@G@@ OTHER B CODE OPERANDS BY CONTEXT.  @[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@         A POINTERWH
)@@G@@ CONTAINS TWO FIELDS: 17 BITS AND 1 BIT. THE 17 @G@@@@ BIT FIELD IS THE WI
)@@G@@ADDRESS AND THE 1 BIT FIELD SIGNIFIES THE H1 PART     @G@@@@ OF THE WORDWJ
)@@G@@ (0) OR THE H2 PART (1). THE ROUTINE SAGBC CONVERTS THE     @G@@@@ CURREWK
)@@G@@NT LOCATION INTO A POINTER, AND THE ROUTINE SAGSBC CONVERTS A     @A@@@@WL
)@@G@@ POINTER TO THE ACTUAL LOCATION.    @]@@@@SPACE 02    @#@@@@2STATEMENT FWM
)@@G@@ORMS  @[@@@@SPACE @G@@@@         EACH STATEMENT IS A STREAM OF TOKENS WHWN
)@@G@@ICH WILL BE DENOTED     @F@@@@ BY THE FOLLOWING BNF-LIKE NOTATION. THE FWO
)@@G@@OLLOWING ADDITIONAL     @ @@@@ CONVENTIONS ARE INCLUDED:    @[@@@@SPACE WP
)@@G@@@C@@@@         [NAME] MEANS THAT NAME IS OPTIONAL.    @D@@@@         ( XWQ
)@@G@@ ! Y ) MEANS THAT X OR Y MUST APPEAR.     @[@@@@SPACE @G@@@@         *NAWR
)@@G@@ME MEANS THAT THE TOKEN NAME BEGINS ON A WORD BOUNDARY.     @D@@@@ IF A WS
)@@G@@TOKEN SPACE HAS TO BE FILLED, ACNIL IS INSERTED.@[@@@@SPACE @G@@@@      WT
)@@G@@   NAME[1] REFERS TO A 9 BIT TOKEN, THE FIRST 9 BITS OF NAME.     @]@@@@WU
)@@G@@SPACE 02    @]@@@@1EXPRESSIONS@[@@@@SPACE @B@@@@         EXPR = ACSTEX[1WV
)@@G@@] D EXP ACENEX    @E@@@@              ( D REFERS TO A 9 BIT FLAG THAT SIWW
)@@G@@GNIFIES     @D@@@@              THE EXPRESSION TYPE. IT CONSISTS OF 3   WX
)@@G@@@D@@@@              ARGUMENTS. ARGUMENT 1 IS TYPE (SCALAR OR@D@@@@      WY
)@@G@@        STRUCTURE), ARGUMENT 2 IS CONTEXT (LHS  @D@@@@              IS LWZ
)@@G@@EFT HAND SIDE (ASSIGNED TO), NTR    @D@@@@              IS ENTRY) AND ARXA
)@@G@@GUMENT 3 IS DATA TYPE   @D@@@@              (STRING, ARITHMETIC, LABEL, XB
)@@G@@ANYTHING))  @F@@@@              SEMA ONLY LOOKS FOR EXPRESSIONS AND THE XC
)@@G@@D DESCRIBES @C@@@@              THE CONTEXT OF THE EXPRESSION.    @B@@@@XD
)@@G@@         EXPRIO = ACSTXI[1] D 0 EXP ACENXI@A@@@@         PEXPR = ACLPAR XE
)@@G@@EXPR ACRPAR @B@@@@         SEXPR = EXPR ! SEXPR ACCOMA  EXPR@A@@@@      XF
